# Task: Debug Query Plan Regression in TiDB Cost-Based Optimizer

## Background
A user reports that after upgrading TiDB, a query that previously used an index scan is now doing a full table scan. The query involves a JOIN between two tables with a WHERE clause on an indexed column.

## Objective
Investigate the cost model in TiDB's query optimizer to identify which component could cause a plan regression where an IndexScan is replaced by a TableFullScan.

## Steps
1. Find the cost model implementation in `pkg/planner/core/` that computes the cost of IndexScan vs TableFullScan
2. Identify the `Stats` struct and how row count estimates feed into the cost calculation
3. Locate where the optimizer compares candidate plans and selects the cheapest
4. Create a file `debug_report.md` in `/workspace/` documenting:
   - The file paths and functions responsible for cost calculation of IndexScan
   - The file paths and functions responsible for cost calculation of TableFullScan
   - The comparison logic that picks the final plan
   - A hypothesis for what parameter change could cause the regression

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/planner/core/` — optimizer core
- `pkg/planner/cardinality/` — cardinality estimation
- `pkg/statistics/` — statistics framework

## Success Criteria
- debug_report.md exists and contains the relevant file paths
- Report identifies cost model functions for both scan types
- Report includes a plausible regression hypothesis

    23→- **TiFlash Startup Penalty:** Added when using TiFlash store type

    32→cost = outCount * GetScanFactor(table) * width

Perfect! I've successfully created a comprehensive debug report documenting the TiDB cost-based optimizer. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Report Summary

**File Created:** `/workspace/debug_report.md`

### Key Components Identified:

1. **IndexScan Cost Calculation**
   - Location: `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go:123-135` 
   - Function: `PhysicalIndexScan.GetPlanCostVer2()`
   - Formula: `cost = rows * log2(row-size) * scan-factor`
   - Also includes seek cost: `+ float64(len(ranges)) * GetSeekFactor()`

2. **TableScan Cost Calculation**
   - Location: `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go:140-170`
   - Function: `PhysicalTableScan.GetPlanCostVer2()`
   - Formula: `cost = rows * log2(row-size) * scan-factor`
   - Includes penalties for TiFlash startup and full scan underestimation

3. **Plan Comparison Logic**
   - Location: `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go:349-364`
   - Function: `compareTaskCost()`
   - Decision: Selects plan with lowest cost (`return curCost < bestCost`)

### Regression Hypothesis (Prioritized):

1. **Row Count Estimation Changes** (HIGH impact) - Most likely cause
2. **Scan Factor Changes** (MEDIUM impact)
3. **Network Factor Changes** (MEDIUM impact)
4. **Cost Model Version Switching** (MEDIUM-HIGH impact)
5. **TiFlash Startup Penalty** (LOW-MEDIUM impact)
6. **Join Selectivity Estimation** (MEDIUM impact)

The report includes detailed debugging steps, a comprehensive file summary table, and explains how parameter changes could cause the regression.

  "content": "# TiDB Cost-Based Optimizer Query Plan Regression Debug Report\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis report investigates the cost model components in TiDB's query optimizer that could cause a query plan regression where an IndexScan is replaced by a TableFullScan after an upgrade.\n\n## Key Findings\n\n### 1. Cost Calculation Components\n\n#### TableScan Cost Model\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go:140-170`\n\n**Function:** `PhysicalTableScan.GetPlanCostVer2()`\n\n**Cost Formula:**\n```\ncost = rows * log2(row-size) * scan-factor\n```\n\n**Additional Penalties:**\n- **TiFlash Startup Penalty:** Added when using TiFlash store type\n- **Full Scan Underestimation Penalty:** Applied to TiKV full table scans to prefer range scans when appropriate\n- **Minimum Row Threshold:** Applied when not a child of IndexLookUp (line 155-156)\n\n**Related Implementation:** `pkg/planner/implementation/datasource.go:126-135`\n\n**Function:** `TableScanImpl.CalcCost()`\n\n```\ncost = outCount * GetScanFactor(table) * width\n# OR if Desc\ncost = outCount * GetDescScanFactor(table) * width\n```\n\n---\n\n#### IndexScan Cost Model\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go:123-135`\n\n**Function:** `PhysicalIndexScan.GetPlanCostVer2()`\n\n**Cost Formula:**\n```\ncost = rows * log2(row-size) * scan-factor\n```\n\n**Related Implementation:** `pkg/planner/implementation/datasource.go:183-194`\n\n**Function:** `IndexScanImpl.CalcCost()`\n\n```\ncost = outCount * rowSize * GetScanFactor(table)\n# OR if Desc\ncost = outCount * rowSize * GetDescScanFactor(table)\n# PLUS seek cost\ncost += float64(len(ranges)) * GetSeekFactor(table)\n```\n\n**Key Difference:** IndexScan includes a **seek cost component** based on the number of ranges in the scan.\n\n---\n\n#### Network Cost Components\n\n**TableReader Cost:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go:248-276`\n\n**Function:** `PhysicalTableReader.GetPlanCostVer1()`\n\n```\ncost = childCost + (rowCount * rowSize * netFactor) / sqlScanConcurrency\n```\n\n**IndexReader Cost:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go:206-237`\n\n**Function:** `PhysicalIndexReader.GetPlanCostVer1()`\n\n```\ncost = childCost + (rowCount * rowSize * netFactor) / sqlScanConcurrency\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. Row Count Estimation (Cardinality)\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go:1248-1250`\n\n**Function:** `getCardinality()`\n\nThe row count feed into cost calculations comes from:\n- **Stats-based estimation** (default): Uses table statistics and selectivity calculations\n- **True cardinality** (with flag): Uses actual row counts from execution\n\n**Key Factors:**\n- Filter conditions and their selectivity\n- Index range bounds\n- Column statistics (histogram, MCV)\n\n---\n\n### 3. Plan Selection Logic\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go:349-364`\n\n**Function:** `compareTaskCost()`\n\n```go\nfunc compareTaskCost(curTask, bestTask base.Task, op *optimizetrace.PhysicalOptimizeOp) (curIsBetter bool, err error) {\n    curCost, curInvalid, err := getTaskPlanCost(curTask, op)\n    bestCost, bestInvalid, err := getTaskPlanCost(bestTask, op)\n    if curInvalid {\n        return false, nil\n    }\n    if bestInvalid {\n        return true, nil\n    }\n    return curCost < bestCost, nil  // Simple cost comparison: lower cost wins\n}\n```\n\n**Decision Rule:** The optimizer selects the plan with the **lowest calculated cost**. If costs are equal, earlier candidates are preferred.\n\n---\n\n## Regression Hypothesis\n\nA query plan regression (IndexScan \u2192 TableFullScan) can occur due to changes in any of the following:\n\n### 1. **Row Count Estimation Changes** \u26a0\ufe0f **MOST LIKELY**\n\n**Impact:** HIGH\n\nWhen row count estimates change significantly, the cost formula is dramatically affected:\n\n```\nOld estimate: 100 rows   \u2192 IndexScan cost = 100 * log2(20) * 0.001 \u2248 0.5\nNew estimate: 100,000 rows \u2192 TableScan cost = 100,000 * log2(30) * 0.0001 \u2248 17\n```\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Statistics update with inaccurate histograms\n- Changes in selectivity calculation (see `pkg/planner/cardinality/`)\n- Filter condition interpretation changes\n- Upgrade to new statistics framework\n\n**Files to Investigate:**\n- `pkg/planner/cardinality/` (selectivity calculation)\n- `pkg/statistics/` (histogram updates)\n- `pkg/planner/core/stats.go` (deriveStats4LogicalTableScan, deriveStats4LogicalIndexScan)\n\n### 2. **Scan Factor Changes**\n\n**Impact:** MEDIUM\n\nThe `GetScanFactor()` and `GetDescScanFactor()` methods in session variables control the relative cost of scanning. Changes in these factors directly multiply row count:\n\n```\nOld factor: 0.001 \u2192 cost = rows * 0.001\nNew factor: 0.01  \u2192 cost = rows * 0.01 (10x more expensive)\n```\n\n**Files to Investigate:**\n- Check session variable initialization in `pkg/sessionctx/variable/`\n- Version-specific cost model adjustments\n\n### 3. **Network Factor Changes**\n\n**Impact:** MEDIUM\n\nThe network cost component can change how TableReader and IndexReader costs are calculated:\n\n```\nTableReader cost = scan_cost + (rows * rowSize * netFactor) / concurrency\nIndexReader cost = scan_cost + (rows * rowSize * netFactor) / concurrency\n```\n\nIf network factor increased significantly, TableReader could become more expensive relative to IndexScan.\n\n### 4. **Cost Model Version Switching**\n\n**Impact:** MEDIUM-HIGH\n\nTiDB has multiple cost models:\n- **Ver1:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` (simpler formula)\n- **Ver2:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` (logarithmic formula: `rows * log2(rowSize) * scanFactor`)\n\nThe cost formula itself is different:\n```\nVer1: cost = rows * rowSize * scanFactor\nVer2: cost = rows * log2(rowSize) * scanFactor  \u2190 Different!\n```\n\nA switch from Ver1 to Ver2 could cause regressions.\n\n### 5. **TiFlash Startup Penalty**\n\n**Impact:** LOW-MEDIUM\n\nLine 164 in `plan_cost_ver2.go`:\n```go\nif p.StoreType == kv.TiFlash {\n    p.PlanCostVer2 = costusage.SumCostVer2(p.PlanCostVer2,\n        scanCostVer2(option, TiFlashStartupRowPenalty, rowSize, scanFactor))\n}\n```\n\nChanges to `TiFlashStartupRowPenalty` constant could affect plan selection.\n\n### 6. **Join Selectivity Estimation**\n\n**Impact:** MEDIUM**\n\nWhen a query involves a JOIN with WHERE clauses:\n- Incorrect join cardinality estimation\n- Selectivity of joined rows differs from estimate\n- Can cause TableScan to appear cheaper if inner table rows are underestimated\n\n---\n\n## Debugging Steps Recommended\n\n1. **Compare Row Count Estimates:**\n   ```sql\n   EXPLAIN SELECT ... \\G  -- Before upgrade\n   EXPLAIN SELECT ... \\G  -- After upgrade\n   ```\n   Look for significant differences in rows column.\n\n2. **Check Cost Model Version:**\n   ```sql\n   SELECT @@tidb_cost_model_version;\n   ```\n\n3. **Inspect Scan Factors:**\n   ```sql\n   SELECT @@tidb_opt_scan_factor, @@tidb_opt_network_factor;\n   ```\n\n4. **Check Table Statistics:**\n   ```sql\n   ANALYZE TABLE table_name;\n   SHOW STATS_HISTOGRAMS;\n   ```\n\n5. **Enable Cost Tracing:**\n   ```sql\n   EXPLAIN FORMAT='cost_trace' SELECT ...;\n   ```\n\n6. **Check for Configuration Changes:**\n   - Session variable defaults\n   - Optimizer fix controls\n\n---\n\n## File Summary Table\n\n| Component | File Path | Key Functions |\n|-----------|-----------|---|\n| **TableScan Cost (Ver2)** | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | `PhysicalTableScan.GetPlanCostVer2()` (line 140) |\n| **IndexScan Cost (Ver2)** | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` | `PhysicalIndexScan.GetPlanCostVer2()` (line 123) |\n| **TableScan Cost (Ver1)** | `pkg/planner/implementation/datasource.go` | `TableScanImpl.CalcCost()` (line 126) |\n| **IndexScan Cost (Ver1)** | `pkg/planner/implementation/datasource.go` | `IndexScanImpl.CalcCost()` (line 183) |\n| **TableReader Cost** | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` | `PhysicalTableReader.GetPlanCostVer1()` (line 248) |\n| **IndexReader Cost** | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` | `PhysicalIndexReader.GetPlanCostVer1()` (line 206) |\n| **Plan Comparison** | `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go` | `compareTaskCost()` (line 349) |\n| **Row Estimation** | `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` | `getCardinality()` (line 1248) |\n| **Stats Derivation** | `pkg/planner/core/stats.go` | `deriveStats4LogicalTableScan()` (line 61), `deriveStats4LogicalIndexScan()` (line 92) |\n| **Selectivity** | `pkg/planner/cardinality/` | Various selectivity estimators |\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe most probable cause of an IndexScan \u2192 TableFullScan regression is **inaccurate row count estimation** leading to an inflated cost calculation for the index access path. The optimizer then selects the seemingly cheaper TableFullScan based on the incorrect cardinality estimates.\n\nThe cost comparison is straightforward (line 364 in find_best_task.go: `return curCost < bestCost`), so focus should be on understanding what changed in row estimation components.\n\n",

Cost Calculation Components\n\n#### TableScan Cost Model\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go:140-170`\n\n**Function:** `PhysicalTableScan.GetPlanCostVer2()`\n\n**Cost Formula:**\n```\ncost = rows * log2(row-size) * scan-factor\n```\n\n**Additional Penalties:**\n- **TiFlash Startup Penalty:** Added when using TiFlash store type\n- **Full Scan Underestimation Penalty:** Applied to TiKV full table scans to prefer range scans when appropriate\n- **Minimum Row Threshold:** Applied when not a child of IndexLookUp (line 155-156)\n\n**Related Implementation:** `pkg/planner/implementation/datasource.go:126-135`\n\n**Function:** `TableScanImpl.CalcCost()`\n\n```\ncost = outCount * GetScanFactor(table) * width\n# OR if Desc\ncost = outCount * GetDescScanFactor(table) * width\n```\n\n---\n\n#### IndexScan Cost Model\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go:123-135`\n\n**Function:** `PhysicalIndexScan.GetPlanCostVer2()`\n\n**Cost Formula:**\n```\ncost = rows * log2(row-size) * scan-factor\n```\n\n**Related Implementation:** `pkg/planner/implementation/datasource.go:183-194`\n\n**Function:** `IndexScanImpl.CalcCost()`\n\n```\ncost = outCount * rowSize * GetScanFactor(table)\n# OR if Desc\ncost = outCount * rowSize * GetDescScanFactor(table)\n# PLUS seek cost\ncost += float64(len(ranges)) * GetSeekFactor(table)\n```\n\n**Key Difference:** IndexScan includes a **seek cost component** based on the number of ranges in the scan.\n\n---\n\n#### Network Cost Components\n\n**TableReader Cost:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go:248-276`\n\n**Function:** `PhysicalTableReader.GetPlanCostVer1()`\n\n```\ncost = childCost + (rowCount * rowSize * netFactor) / sqlScanConcurrency\n```\n\n**IndexReader Cost:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go:206-237`\n\n**Function:** `PhysicalIndexReader.GetPlanCostVer1()`\n\n```\ncost = childCost + (rowCount * rowSize * netFactor) / sqlScanConcurrency\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. Row Count Estimation (Cardinality)\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go:1248-1250`\n\n**Function:** `getCardinality()`\n\nThe row count feed into cost calculations comes from:\n- **Stats-based estimation** (default): Uses table statistics and selectivity calculations\n- **True cardinality** (with flag): Uses actual row counts from execution\n\n**Key Factors:**\n- Filter conditions and their selectivity\n- Index range bounds\n- Column statistics (histogram, MCV)\n\n---\n\n### 3. Plan Selection Logic\n\n**File:** `pkg/planner/core/find_best_task.go:349-364`\n\n**Function:** `compareTaskCost()`\n\n```go\nfunc compareTaskCost(curTask, bestTask base.Task, op *optimizetrace.PhysicalOptimizeOp) (curIsBetter bool, err error) {\n    curCost, curInvalid, err := getTaskPlanCost(curTask, op)\n    bestCost, bestInvalid, err := getTaskPlanCost(bestTask, op)\n    if curInvalid {\n        return false, nil\n    }\n    if bestInvalid {\n        return true, nil\n    }\n    return curCost < bestCost, nil  // Simple cost comparison: lower cost wins\n}\n```\n\n**Decision Rule:** The optimizer selects the plan with the **lowest calculated cost**. If costs are equal, earlier candidates are preferred.\n\n---\n\n## Regression Hypothesis\n\nA query plan regression (IndexScan \u2192 TableFullScan) can occur due to changes in any of the following:\n\n### 1. **Row Count Estimation Changes** \u26a0\ufe0f **MOST LIKELY**\n\n**Impact:** HIGH\n\nWhen row count estimates change significantly, the cost formula is dramatically affected:\n\n```\nOld estimate: 100 rows   \u2192 IndexScan cost = 100 * log2(20) * 0.001 \u2248 0.5\nNew estimate: 100,000 rows \u2192 TableScan cost = 100,000 * log2(30) * 0.0001 \u2248 17\n```\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Statistics update with inaccurate histograms\n- Changes in selectivity calculation (see `pkg/planner/cardinality/`)\n- Filter condition interpretation changes\n- Upgrade to new statistics framework\n\n**Files to Investigate:**\n- `pkg/planner/cardinality/` (selectivity calculation)\n- `pkg/statistics/` (histogram updates)\n- `pkg/planner/core/stats.go` (deriveStats4LogicalTableScan, deriveStats4LogicalIndexScan)\n\n### 2. **Scan Factor Changes**\n\n**Impact:** MEDIUM\n\nThe `GetScanFactor()` and `GetDescScanFactor()` methods in session variables control the relative cost of scanning. Changes in these factors directly multiply row count:\n\n```\nOld factor: 0.001 \u2192 cost = rows * 0.001\nNew factor: 0.01  \u2192 cost = rows * 0.01 (10x more expensive)\n```\n\n**Files to Investigate:**\n- Check session variable initialization in `pkg/sessionctx/variable/`\n- Version-specific cost model adjustments\n\n### 3. **Network Factor Changes**\n\n**Impact:** MEDIUM\n\nThe network cost component can change how TableReader and IndexReader costs are calculated:\n\n```\nTableReader cost = scan_cost + (rows * rowSize * netFactor) / concurrency\nIndexReader cost = scan_cost + (rows * rowSize * netFactor) / concurrency\n```\n\nIf network factor increased significantly, TableReader could become more expensive relative to IndexScan.\n\n### 4. **Cost Model Version Switching**\n\n**Impact:** MEDIUM-HIGH\n\nTiDB has multiple cost models:\n- **Ver1:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go` (simpler formula)\n- **Ver2:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go` (logarithmic formula: `rows * log2(rowSize) * scanFactor`)\n\nThe cost formula itself is different:\n```\nVer1: cost = rows * rowSize * scanFactor\nVer2: cost = rows * log2(rowSize) * scanFactor  \u2190 Different!\n```\n\nA switch from Ver1 to Ver2 could cause regressions.\n\n### 5. **TiFlash Startup Penalty**\n\n**Impact:** LOW-MEDIUM\n\nLine 164 in `plan_cost_ver2.go`:\n```go\nif p.StoreType == kv.TiFlash {\n    p.PlanCostVer2 = costusage.SumCostVer2(p.PlanCostVer2,\n        scanCostVer2(option, TiFlashStartupRowPenalty, rowSize, scanFactor))\n}\n```\n\nChanges to `TiFlashStartupRowPenalty` constant could affect plan selection.\n\n### 6. **Join Selectivity Estimation**\n\n**Impact:** MEDIUM**\n\nWhen a query involves a JOIN with WHERE clauses:\n- Incorrect join cardinality estimation\n- Selectivity of joined rows differs from estimate\n- Can cause TableScan to appear cheaper if inner table rows are underestimated\n\n---\n\n## Debugging Steps Recommended\n\n1. **Compare Row Count Estimates:**\n   ```sql\n   EXPLAIN SELECT ... \\G  -- Before upgrade\n   EXPLAIN SELECT ... \\G  -- After upgrade\n   ```\n   Look for significant differences in 1. WRITE /workspace/debug_report.md
# TiDB Cost-Based Optimizer Query Plan Regression Debug Report

## Executive Summary

This report investigates the cost model components in TiDB's query optimizer that could cause a query plan regression where an IndexScan is replaced by a TableFullScan after an upgrade.

## Key Findings

### 1. Cost Calculation Components

#### TableScan Cost Model

**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go:140-170`

**Function:** `PhysicalTableScan.GetPlanCostVer2()`

**Cost Formula:**
```
cost = rows * log2(row-size) * scan-factor
```

**Additional Penalties:**
- **TiFlash Startup Penalty:** Added when using TiFlash store type
- **Full Scan Underestimation Penalty:** Applied to TiKV full table scans to prefer range scans when appropriate
- **Minimum Row Threshold:** Applied when not a child of IndexLookUp (line 155-156)

**Related Implementation:** `pkg/planner/implementation/datasource.go:126-135`

**Function:** `TableScanImpl.CalcCost()`

```
cost = outCount * GetScanFactor(table) * width
# OR if Desc
cost = outCount * GetDescScanFactor(table) * width
```

---

#### IndexScan Cost Model

**File:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver2.go:123-135`

**Function:** `PhysicalIndexScan.GetPlanCostVer2()`

**Cost Formula:**
```
cost = rows * log2(row-size) * scan-factor
```

**Related Implementation:** `pkg/planner/implementation/datasource.go:183-194`

**Function:** `IndexScanImpl.CalcCost()`

```
cost = outCount * rowSize * GetScanFactor(table)
# OR if Desc
cost = outCount * rowSize * GetDescScanFactor(table)
# PLUS seek cost
cost += float64(len(ranges)) * GetSeekFactor(table)
```

**Key Difference:** IndexScan includes a **seek cost component** based on the number of ranges in the scan.

---

#### Network Cost Components

**TableReader Cost:** `pkg/planner/core/plan_cost_ver1.go:248-276
... (truncated)

No bash commands parsed.
